#c 2638060 2019-07-03 17:45:47
[Angry Eve] The health benefits of vegetarian diets are not unique. Prudent plant-based dietary patterns which also allow small intakes of red meat, fish and dairy products have demonstrated significant improvements in health status as well. At this time an optimal dietary intake for health status is unknown. Plant-based diets contain a host of food and nutrients known to have independent health benefits. While vegetarian diets have not shown any adverse effects on health, restrictive and monotonous vegetarian diets may result in nutrient deficiencies with deleterious effects on health. â€”â€”McEvoy, Claire T., Norman Temple, and Jayne V. Woodside. "Vegetarian diets, low-meat diets and health: a review." Public health nutrition 15.12 (2012): 2287-2294.
